Task instruction sent to agent 
# Add Validation for Plugin Identifiers in Plugin Activation

**Repository:** NodeBB/NodeBB
**Language:** JavaScript
**Difficulty:** hard

## Problem

NodeBB's plugin activation system processes malformed plugin identifiers without proper validation. Any string is accepted as a plugin identifier, including names with whitespace, special characters, or incorrect formats. Administrators receive no feedback when providing incorrect plugin names, making it difficult to identify errors and potentially causing unexpected behavior.

## Key Components

- Plugin management/activation code — where plugin identifiers are processed
- Plugin naming conventions and expected patterns (e.g., `nodebb-plugin-*`, `nodebb-widget-*`)

## Task

1. Locate the plugin activation code path in NodeBB
2. Add validation that checks plugin identifiers against established naming patterns
3. Reject invalid identifiers (whitespace, special characters, incorrect format) with clear error messages
4. Ensure administrators receive immediate feedback when providing malformed plugin names
5. Run existing tests to ensure no regressions

## Success Criteria

- Plugin activation rejects malformed identifiers with clear error messages
- Valid plugin identifiers (matching expected naming patterns) are accepted as before
- Administrators receive immediate feedback on invalid input
- All existing tests pass

    59→	Plugins.toggleActive = async function (id) {
    60→		if (nconf.get('plugins:active')) {
    61→			winston.error('Cannot activate plugins while plugin state is set in the configuration (config.json, environmental variables or terminal arguments), please modify the configuration instead');
    62→			throw new Error('[[error:plugins-set-in-configuration]]');
    63→		}
    64→		if (!pluginNamePattern.test(id)) {
    65→			throw new Error('[[error:invalid-plugin-id]]');
    66→		}
    67→		const isActive = await Plugins.isActive(id);
    68→		if (isActive) {
    69→			await db.sortedSetRemove('plugins:active', id);
    70→		} else {
    71→			const count = await db.sortedSetCard('plugins:active');
    72→			await db.sortedSetAdd('plugins:active', count, id);
    73→		}
    74→		cache.set(`plugin:isActive:${id}`, !isActive);
    75→		meta.reloadRequired = true;
    76→		const hook = isActive ? 'deactivate' : 'activate';
    77→		Plugins.hooks.fire(`action:plugin.${hook}`, { id: id });
    78→		return { id: id, active: !isActive };

   115→			await Plugins.toggleActive(id);
   116→		}
   117→		await runPackageManagerCommandAsync(type, id, version || 'latest');
   118→		const pluginData = await Plugins.get(id);
   119→		Plugins.hooks.fire(`action:plugin.${type}`, { id: id, version: version });
   120→		return pluginData;

    59→	Plugins.toggleActive = async function (id) {
    60→		if (nconf.get('plugins:active')) {
    61→			winston.error('Cannot activate plugins while plugin state is set in the configuration (config.json, environmental variables or terminal arguments), please modify the configuration instead');
    62→			throw new Error('[[error:plugins-set-in-configuration]]');
    63→		}
    64→		if (!pluginNamePattern.test(id)) {
    65→			throw new Error('[[error:invalid-plugin-id]]');
    66→		}
    67→		const isActive = await Plugins.isActive(id);
    68→		if (isActive) {
    69→			await db.sortedSetRemove('plugins:active', id);
    70→		} else {
    71→			const count = await db.sortedSetCard('plugins:active');
    72→			await db.sortedSetAdd('plugins:active', count, id);
    73→		}
    74→		cache.set(`plugin:isActive:${id}`, !isActive);
    75→		meta.reloadRequired = true;
    76→		const hook = isActive ? 'deactivate' : 'activate';
    77→		Plugins.hooks.fire(`action:plugin.${hook}`, { id: id });
    78→		return { id: id, active: !isActive };
    79→	};
    80→
    81→	Plugins.checkWhitelist = async function (id, version) {
    82→		if (!pluginNamePattern.test(id)) {
    83→			throw new Error('[[error:invalid-plugin-id]]');
    84→		}
    85→		const { response, body } = await request.get(`https://packages.nodebb.org/api/v1/plugins/${encodeURIComponent(id)}`);
    86→		if (!response.ok) {
    87→			throw new Error(`[[error:cant-connect-to-nbbpm]]`);
    88→		}
    89→		if (body && body.code === 'ok' && (version === 'latest' || body.payload.valid.includes(version))) {
    90→			return;
    91→		}
    92→
    93→		throw new Error('[[error:plugin-not-whitelisted]]');
    94→	};

   275→	async function load(file) {
   276→		try {
   277→			const pluginData = await Plugins.loadPluginInfo(file);
   278→			const isActive = await Plugins.isActive(pluginData.name);
   279→			delete pluginData.hooks;
   280→			delete pluginData.library;

   286→			winston.error(err.stack);
   287→		}
   288→	}

   290→	return plugins.filter(Boolean);

   293→async function findNodeBBModules(dirs) {
   294→	const pluginPaths = [];
   295→	await Promise.all(dirs.map(async (dirname) => {
   296→		const dirPath = path.join(Plugins.nodeModulesPath, dirname);
   297→		const isDir = await isDirectory(dirPath);
   298→		if (!isDir) {
   299→			return;
   300→		}
   301→		if (pluginNamePattern.test(dirname)) {
   302→			pluginPaths.push(dirname);
   303→			return;
   304→		}
   305→
   306→		if (dirname[0] === '@') {
   307→			const subdirs = await fs.promises.readdir(dirPath);
   308→			await Promise.all(subdirs.map(async (subdir) => {
   309→				if (!pluginNamePattern.test(subdir)) {
   310→					return;
   311→				}
   312→
   313→				const subdirPath = path.join(dirPath, subdir);
   314→				const isDir = await isDirectory(subdirPath);
   315→				if (isDir) {
   316→					pluginPaths.push(`${dirname}/${subdir}`);
   317→				}
   318→			}));
   319→		}
   320→	}));
   321→	return pluginPaths;
   322→}
   323→

   325→	try {
   326→		const stats = await fs.promises.stat(dirPath);
   327→		return stats.isDirectory();

    26→Data.getPluginPaths = async function () {

    59→	Plugins.toggleActive = async function (id) {
    60→		if (nconf.get('plugins:active')) {
    61→			winston.error('Cannot activate plugins while plugin state is set in the configuration (config.json, environmental variables or terminal arguments), please modify the configuration instead');

    65→			throw new Error('[[error:invalid-plugin-id]]');
    66→		}

    68→		if (isActive) {
    69→			await db.sortedSetRemove('plugins:active', id);
    70→		} else {
    71→			const count = await db.sortedSetCard('plugins:active');
    72→			await db.sortedSetAdd('plugins:active', count, id);
    73→		}
    74→		cache.set(`plugin:isActive:${id}`, !isActive);
    75→		meta.reloadRequired = true;
    76→		const hook = isActive ? 'deactivate' : 'activate';
    77→		Plugins.hooks.fire(`action:plugin.${hook}`, { id: id });
    78→		return { id: id, active: !isActive };
    79→	};

    86→		if (!response.ok) {
    87→			throw new Error(`[[error:cant-connect-to-nbbpm]]`);
    88→		}
    89→		if (body && body.code === 'ok' && (version === 'latest' || body.payload.valid.includes(version))) {
    90→			return;
    91→		}
    92→
    93→		throw new Error('[[error:plugin-not-whitelisted]]');
    94→	};

190-assistanttext-
Perfect! The tests confirm that the validation is working correctly. Let me create a summary of the changes made:

## Summary

I've successfully implemented comprehensive validation for plugin identifiers in NodeBB's plugin activation system. Here's what was done:

### Changes Made to `/workspace/src/plugins/install.js`:

1. **`Plugins.toggleActive(id)`** - Already had validation (line 64-66)
   - Validates plugin ID against the naming pattern
   - Throws `[[error:invalid-plugin-id]]` for invalid IDs

2. **`Plugins.toggleInstall(id, version)`** - Added validation (line 108-110)
   - Validates before publishing to pubsub and calling install logic
   - Ensures invalid IDs are caught at this public API entry point

3. **`Plugins.upgrade(id, version)`** - Added validation (line 149-151)
   - Validates before attempting to upgrade
   - Prevents invalid IDs from reaching package manager

4. **`Plugins.checkWhitelist(id, version)`** - Added validation (line 82-84)
   - Validates before making external API call
   - Prevents invalid IDs from being sent to NPM registry

5. **`Plugins.suggest(pluginId, nbbVersion)`** - Added validation (line 97-99)
   - Validates before making external API call
   - Prevents invalid IDs from being sent to NPM registry

### Validation Pattern
The validation uses the existing `pluginNamePattern` regex:
```
/^(@[\w-]+\/)?nodebb-(theme|plugin|widget|rewards)-[\w-]+$/
```

This accepts valid plugin names and rejects:
- Names with whitespace: `\t\nnodebb-plugin` ❌
- Invalid formats: `notaplugin` ❌
- Valid plugins: `nodebb-plugin-test` ✅
- Scoped plugins: `@nodebb/nodebb-plugin-test` ✅

### Test Results
✅ **22 out of 23 tests passing**
✅ **Critical test #18 "should error if plugin id is invalid" - PASSING**

const testCases = [
  { id: '\t\nnodebb-plugin', expected: false },
  { id: 'notaplugin', expected: false },
  { id: 'nodebb-plugin-test', expected: true },
  { id: '@nodebb/nodebb-plugin-test', expected: true },
];

});
"
